Having proved a preservation property in the last chapter, a natural
next step would be to prove progress. That is, to prove a property
of the form

    If Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v, then either M is a lambda abstraction or M ‚Äî‚Üí N for some N.

Such a property would tell us that having a denotation implies either
reduction to normal form or divergence. This is indeed true, but we
can prove a much stronger property! In fact, having a denotation that
is a function value (not `‚ä•`) implies reduction to a lambda
abstraction (no divergence).

This stronger property, reformulated a bit, is known as _adequacy_.
That is, if a term `M` is denotationally equal to a lambda abstraction,
then `M` reduces to a lambda abstraction.

    ‚Ñ∞ M ‚âÉ ‚Ñ∞ (∆õ N)  implies M ‚Äî‚Ü† ∆õ N' for some N'

Recall that `‚Ñ∞ M ‚âÉ ‚Ñ∞ (∆õ N)` is equivalent to saying that
`Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì (v ‚Ü¶ w)` for some `v` and `w`. We will show that
`Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì (v ‚Ü¶ w)` implies reduction a lambda abstraction.

It is well known that a term can reduce to a lambda abstraction using
full Œ≤ reduction if and only if it can reduce to a lambda abstraction
using the call-by-name reduction strategy. So we shall prove that
`Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì (v ‚Ü¶ w)` implies that `M` halts under call-by-name evaluation,
which we define with a big-step semantics written `Œ≥' ‚ä¢ M ‚áì c`, where
`c` is a closure (a term paired with an environment) and `Œ≥'` is an
environment that maps variables to closures

So we will show that `Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì (v ‚Ü¶ w)` implies `Œ≥' ‚ä¢ M ‚áì c`,
provided `Œ≥` and `Œ≥'` are appropriate related.  The proof will
be an induction on the derivation of `Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v`, and to
strengthen the induction hypothesis, we will relate semantic values to
closures using a _logical relation_ `ùïç`.

The rest of this chapter is organized as follows.

* We loosen the requirement that `M` result in a function value and
  instead require that `M` result in a value that is greater than or
  equal to a function value. We establish several properties about
  being ``greater than a function''.

* We define the call-by-name big-step semantics of the lambda calculus
  and prove that it is deterministic.

* We define the logical relation `ùïç` that relates values and closures,
  and extend it to a relation on terms `ùîº` and environments `ùîæ`.

* We prove the main lemma,
  that if `ùîæ Œ≥ Œ≥'` and `Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v`, then `ùîº v (clos M Œ≥')`.

* We prove adequacy as a corollary to the main lemma.


## The property of being greater or equal to a function

We define the following short-hand for saying that a value is
greather-than or equal to a function value.

If a value `u` is greater than a function, then an even greater value `u'`
is too.

The bottom value `‚ä•` is not greater than a function.

class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a> <a id="3906" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a> <a id="3908" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a>
    <a id="3914" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="3919" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#31410" class="Function">Funs‚àà</a> <a id="3925" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3878" class="Bound">f</a>
<a id="3927" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="3931" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="3933" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü®</a> <a id="3935" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3935" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3937" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="3939" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü®</a> <a id="3941" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3941" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="3943" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="3945" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3945" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="3947" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a> <a id="3949" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a>
    <a id="3955" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="3960" class="Bound">Œì‚äÜ‚ä•</a> <a id="3964" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3945" class="Bound">m</a>
<a id="3966" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="3970" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="3972" class="Symbol">()</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

If the join of two values `u` and `u'` is greater than a function, then
at least one of them is too.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="AboveFun-‚äî"></a><a id="4102" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4102" class="Function">AboveFun-‚äî</a> <a id="4113" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4115" class="Symbol">‚àÄ{</a><a id="4117" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4117" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4119" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4119" class="Bound">u&#39;</a><a id="4121" class="Symbol">}</a>

On the other hand, if neither of `u` and `u'` is greater than a function,
then their join is also not greater than a function.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="not-AboveFun-‚äî"></a><a id="4615" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4615" class="Function">not-AboveFun-‚äî</a> <a id="4630" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4632" class="Symbol">‚àÄ{</a><a id="4634" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4634" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4636" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4636" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="4639" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4641" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="4646" class="Symbol">}</a>
               <a id="4663" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="4665" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬¨</a> <a id="4667" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3351" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4676" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4634" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4678" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="4680" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬¨</a> <a id="4682" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3351" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4691" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4636" class="Bound">u&#39;</a>
               <a id="4709" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="4711" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬¨</a> <a id="4713" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3351" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4722" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4723" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4634" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4725" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4159" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚äî</a> <a id="4727" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4636" class="Bound">u&#39;</a><a id="4729" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="4731" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4615" class="Function">not-AboveFun-‚äî</a> <a id="4746" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4746" class="Bound">naf1</a> <a id="4751" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4751" class="Bound">naf2</a> <a id="4756" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4756" class="Bound">af12</a>
    <a id="4765" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="4770" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4102" class="Function">AboveFun-‚äî</a> <a id="4781" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4756" class="Bound">af12</a>
<a id="4786" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="4790" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="4792" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">inj‚ÇÅ</a> <a id="4797" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4797" class="Bound">af1</a> <a id="4801" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4803" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="4817" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4797" class="Bound">af1</a> <a id="4821" class="Bound">naf1</a>
<a id="4826" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="4830" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="4832" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">inj‚ÇÇ</a> <a id="4837" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4837" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="4841" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4843" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="4857" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4837" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="4861" class="Bound">naf2</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The converse is also true. If the join of two values is not above a
function, then neither of them is individually.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="not-AboveFun-‚äî-inv"></a><a id="5008" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5008" class="Function">not-AboveFun-‚äî-inv</a> <a id="5027" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5029" class="Symbol">‚àÄ{</a><a id="5031" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5031" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5033" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5033" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="5036" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5038" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="5043" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5045" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="5047" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬¨</a> <a id="5049" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3351" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5058" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5059" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5031" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5061" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4159" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚äî</a> <a id="5063" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5033" class="Bound">u&#39;</a><a id="5065" class="Symbol">)</a>

The property of being greater than a function value is decidable, as
exhibited by the following function.

## Big-step semantics for call-by-name lambda calculus

To better align with the denotational semantics, we shall use an
environment-passing big-step semantics. Because this is call-by-name,
an environment maps each variable to a closure, that is, to a term
paired with its environment. (Environments and closures are mutually
recursive.) We define environments and closures as follows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ClosEnv"></a><a id="6369" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6369" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="6377" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6379" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2980" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="6387" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="6389" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>

<a id="6394" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Clos"></a><a id="6399" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6399" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="6404" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6406" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="6410" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="Clos.clos"></a><a id="6418" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6418" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="6423" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6425" class="Symbol">‚àÄ{</a><a id="6427" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6427" class="Bound">Œì</a><a id="6428" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6430" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="6432" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6433" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6433" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="6435" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6437" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6427" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="6439" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">‚ä¢</a> <a id="6441" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">‚òÖ</a><a id="6442" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6444" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="6446" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6369" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="6454" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6427" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="6456" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="6458" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6399" class="Datatype">Clos</a>

<a id="6464" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6369" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="6472" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6472" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="6474" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6476" class="Symbol">‚àÄ</a> <a id="6478" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6479" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6479" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6481" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6483" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6472" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="6485" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3365" class="Datatype Operator">‚àã</a> <a id="6487" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">‚òÖ</a><a id="6488" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6490" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="6492" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6399" class="Datatype">Clos</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

As usual, we have the empty environment, and we can extend an
environment.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="‚àÖ&#39;"></a><a id="6597" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6597" class="Function">‚àÖ&#39;</a> <a id="6600" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6602" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6369" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="6610" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3002" class="InductiveConstructor">‚àÖ</a>

<a id="6684" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6685" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6685" class="Bound">Œ≥</a> <a id="6687" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6619" class="Function Operator">,&#39;</a> <a id="6690" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6690" class="Bound">c</a><a id="6691" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6693" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6694" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3446" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S</a> <a id="6696" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6696" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6697" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6699" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6701" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6685" class="Bound">Œ≥</a> <a id="6703" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6696" class="Bound">x</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The following is the big-step semantics for call-by-name evaluation,
which we describe below.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="6825" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="_‚ä¢_‚áì_"></a><a id="6830" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6830" class="Datatype Operator">_‚ä¢_‚áì_</a> <a id="6836" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6838" class="Symbol">‚àÄ{</a><a id="6840" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6840" class="Bound">Œì</a><a id="6841" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6843" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="6845" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6369" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="6853" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6840" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="6855" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="6857" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6858" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6840" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="6860" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">‚ä¢</a> <a id="6862" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">‚òÖ</a><a id="6863" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6865" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="6867" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6399" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="6872" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="6874" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="6878" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="_‚ä¢_‚áì_.‚áì-var"></a><a id="6887" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6887" class="InductiveConstructor">‚áì-var</a> <a id="6893"         <a id="6966" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="6968" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6900" class="Bound">Œ≥</a> <a id="6970" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6915" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6972" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">‚â°</a> <a id="6974" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6418" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="6979" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6944" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="6981" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6929" class="Bound">Œ¥</a>
        <a id="6991" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="6993" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6929" class="Bound">Œ¥</a> <a id="6995" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6830" class="Datatype Operator">‚ä¢</a> <a id="6997" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6944" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="6999" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6830" class="Datatype Operator">‚áì</a> <a id="7001" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6955" class="Bound">c</a>
          <a id="7013" class="Comment">-----------</a>

class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7253" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7159" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="7255" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl class="Datatype Operator">‚ä¢</a> <a id="7260" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7188" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="7262" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl          <a id="7275" class="Comment">----------------------------------------------------</a>
       <a id="7335" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="7337" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7142" class="Bound">Œ≥</a> <a id="7339" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6830" class="Datatype Operator">‚ä¢</a> <a id="7341" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7157" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="7343" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬∑</a> <a id="7345" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7159" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="7347" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6830" class="Datatype Operator">‚áì</a> <a id="7349" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7203" class="Bound">c</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* The `‚áì-var` rule evaluates a variable by finding the associated
  closure in the environment and then evaluating the closure.

* The `‚áì-lam` rule turns a lambda abstraction into a closure
  by packaging it up with its environment.

* The `‚áì-app` rule performs function application by first evaluating
  the term `L` in operator position. If that produces a closure containing
  a lambda abstraction `∆õ N`, then we evaluate the body `N` in an
  environment extended with the argument `M`. Note that `M` is not
  evaluated in rule `‚áì-app` because this is call-by-name and not
  call-by-value.

If the big-step semantics says that a term `M` evaluates to both `c` and
`c'`, then `c` and `c'` are identical. In other words, the big-step relation
is a partial function.

<a id="8446" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="8450" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="8452" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="8457" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8459" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8144" class="Function">‚áì-determ</a> <a id="8468" class="Bound">mc‚ÇÅ</a> <a id="8472" class="Bound">mc&#39;&#39;</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Relating values to closures

Next we relate semantic values to closures.  The relation `ùïç` is for
closures whose term is a lambda abstraction, i.e., in weak-head normal
form (WHNF). The relation ùîº is for any closure. Roughly speaking,
`ùîº v c` will hold if, when `v` is greater than a function value, `c` evaluates
to a closure `c'` in WHNF and `ùïç v c'`. Regarding `ùïç v c`, it will hold when
`c` is in WHNF, and if `v` is a function, the body of `c` evaluates
according to `v`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ùïç"></a><a id="8984" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8984" class="Function">ùïç</a> <a id="8986" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8988" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="8994" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="8996" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6399" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="9001" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="9003" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="ùîº"></a><a id="9007" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9007" class="Function">ùîº</a> <a id="9009" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9011" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="9017" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="9019" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6399" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="9024" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="9026" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We define `ùïç` as a function from values and closures to `Set` and not as a
data type because it is mutually recursive with `ùîº` in a negative
position (to the left of an implication).  We first perform case
analysis on the term in the closure. If the term is a variable or
application, then `ùïç` is false (`Bot`). If the term is a lambda
abstraction, we define `ùïç` by recursion on the value, which we
describe below.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="9471" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8984" class="Function">ùïç</a> <a id="9473" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9473" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="9475" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9476" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6418" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="9481" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9482" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4186" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="9484" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9484" class="Bound">x‚ÇÅ</a><a id="9486" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9488" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9488" class="Bound">Œ≥</a><a id="9489" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9491" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9493" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Empty.html#243" class="Datatype">Bot</a>
<a id="9497" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8984" class="Function">ùïç</a> <a id="9499" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9499" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="9501" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9502" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6418" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="9507" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9508" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9508" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="9510" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬∑</a> <a id="9512" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9512" class="Bound">M‚ÇÅ</a><a id="9514" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9516" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9516" class="Bound">Œ≥</a><a id="9517" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9519" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9521" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Empty.html#243" class="Datatype">Bot</a>
<a id="9525" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8984" class="Function">ùïç</a> <a id="9527" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4117" class="InductiveConstructor">‚ä•</a> <a id="9529" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9530" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6418" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="9535" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9536" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∆õ</a> <a id="9538" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9538" class="Bound">M</a><a id="9539" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9541" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9541" class="Bound">Œ≥</a><a id="9542" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9544" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9546" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Unit.html#69" class="Record">‚ä§</a>
<a id="9548" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8984" class="Function">ùïç</a> <a id="9550" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9551" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9551" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="9553" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚Ü¶</a> <a id="9555" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9555" class="Bound">w</a><a id="9556" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9558" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9559" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6418" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="9564" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9565" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∆õ</a> <a id="9567" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9567" class="Bound">N</a><a id="9568" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9570" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9570" class="Bound">Œ≥</a><a id="9571" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9573" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="9579" class="Symbol">(‚àÄ{</a><a id="9582" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9582" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="9584" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9586" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6399" class="Datatype">Clos</a><a id="9590" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9592" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="9594" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9007" class="Function">ùîº</a> <a id="9596" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9551" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="9598" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9582" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="9600" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="9602" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3351" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="9611" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9555" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="9613" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="9615" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">Œ£[</a> <a id="9618" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9618" class="Bound">c&#39;</a> <a id="9621" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">‚àà</a> <a id="9623" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6399" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="9628" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">]</a>
        <a id="9638" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9639" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9570" class="Bound">Œ≥</a> <a id="9641" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6619" class="Function Operator">,&#39;</a> <a id="9644" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9582" class="Bound">c</a><a id="9645" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9647" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6830" class="Datatype Operator">‚ä¢</a> <a id="9649" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9567" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="9651" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6830" class="Datatype Operator">‚áì</a> <a id="9653" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9618" class="Bound">c&#39;</a>  <a id="9657" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">√ó</a>  <a id="9660" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8984" class="Function">ùïç</a> <a id="9662" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9555" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="9664" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9618" class="Bound">c&#39;</a><a id="9666" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="9668" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8984" class="Function">ùïç</a> <a id="9670" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9671" href="{% endraw %}{{ class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚äî</a> <a id="9675" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9675" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9676" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9678" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9679" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6418" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="9684" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9685" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∆õ</a> <a id="9687" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9687" class="Bound">N</a><a id="9688" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9690" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9690" class="Bound">Œ≥</a><a id="9691" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9693" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9695" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8984" class="Function">ùïç</a> <a id="9697" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9671" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="9699" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9700" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6418" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="9705" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9706" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∆õ</a> <a id="9708" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9687" class="Bound">N</a><a id="9709" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9711" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9690" class="Bound">Œ≥</a><a id="9712" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9714" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">√ó</a> <a id="9716" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8984" class="Function">ùïç</a> <a id="9718" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9675" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="9720" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9721" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6418" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="9726" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9727" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∆õ</a> <a id="9729" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9687" class="Bound">N</a><a id="9730" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9732" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9690" class="Bound">Œ≥</a><a id="9733" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* If the value is `‚ä•`, then the result is true (`‚ä§`).

* If the value is a join (u ‚äî v), then the result is the pair
  (conjunction) of ùïç is true for both u and v.

* The important case is for a function value `v ‚Ü¶ w` and closure
  `clos (∆õ N) Œ≥`. Given any closure `c` such that `ùîº v c`, if `w` is
  greater than a function, then `N` evaluates (with `Œ≥` extended with `c`)
  to some closure `c'` and we have `ùïç w c'`.


The definition of `ùîº` is straightforward. If `v` is a greater than a
function, then `M` evaluates to a closure related to `v`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10309" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9007" class="Function">ùîº</a> <a id="10311" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10311" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="10313" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10314" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6418" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="10319" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10319" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="10321" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10321" class="Bound">Œ≥&#39;</a><a id="10323" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10325" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10327" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3351" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="10336" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10311" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="10338" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="10340" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">Œ£[</a> <a id="10343" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10343" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="10345" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">‚àà</a> <a id="10347" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6399" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="10352" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">]</a> <a id="10354" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10321" class="Bound">Œ≥&#39;</a> <a id="10357" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6830" class="Datatype Operator">‚ä¢</a> <a id="10359" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10319" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="10361" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6830" class="Datatype Operator">‚áì</a> <a id="10363" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10343" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="10365" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">√ó</a> <a id="10367" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8984" class="Function">ùïç</a> <a id="10369" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10311" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="10371" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10343" class="Bound">c</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof of the main lemma is by induction on `Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v`, so it goes
underneath lambda abstractions and must therefore reason about open
terms (terms with variables). So we must relate environments of
semantic values to environments of closures.  In the following, `ùîæ`
relates `Œ≥` to `Œ≥'` if the corresponding values and closures are related
by `ùîº`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ùîæ"></a><a id="10751" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10751" class="Function">ùîæ</a> <a id="10753" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10755" class="Symbol">‚àÄ{</a><a id="10757" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10757" class="Bound">Œì</a><a id="10758" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10760" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="10762" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7331" class="Function">Env</a> <a id="10766" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10757" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="10768" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="10770" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6369" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="10778" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10757" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="10780" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="10782" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>

We need a few properties of the `ùïç` and `ùîº` relations.  The first is that
a closure in the `ùïç` relation must be in weak-head normal form.  We
define WHNF has follows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="11203" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="WHNF"></a><a id="11208" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11208" class="Datatype">WHNF</a> <a id="11213" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11215" class="Symbol">‚àÄ</a> <a id="11217" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11218" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11218" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="11220" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11220" class="Bound">A</a><a id="11221" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11223" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="11225" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11218" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="11227" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">‚ä¢</a> <a id="11229" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11220" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="11231" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="11233" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="11237" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="WHNF.∆õ_"></a><a id="11245" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11245" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∆õ_</a> <a id="11248" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11250" class="Symbol">‚àÄ</a> <a id="11252" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11253" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11253" class="Bound">Œì</a><a id="11254" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11256" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11257" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11257" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="11259" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11261" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11253" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="11263" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="11265" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">‚òÖ</a> <a id="11267" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">‚ä¢</a> <a id="11269" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">‚òÖ</a><a id="11270" class="Symbol">}</a>
     <a id="11277" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="11279" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11208" class="Datatype">WHNF</a> <a id="11284" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11285" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∆õ</a> <a id="11287" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11257" class="Bound">N</a><a id="11288" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof goes by cases on the term in the closure.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ùïç‚ÜíWHNF"></a><a id="11368" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11368" class="Function">ùïç‚ÜíWHNF</a> <a id="11375" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11377" class="Symbol">‚àÄ{</a><a id="11379" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11379" class="Bound">Œì</a><a id="11380" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="11382" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11382" class="Bound">Œ≥</a> <a id="11384" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11386" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6369" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="11394" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11379" class="Bound">Œì</a><a id="11395" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="11397" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11397" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="11399" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11401" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11379" class="Bound">Œì</a> <a id="11403" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">‚ä¢</a> <a id="11405" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">‚òÖ</a><a id="11406" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="11408" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11408" class="Bound">v</a><a id="11409" class="Symbol">}</a>
       <a id="11418" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="11420" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8984" class="Function">ùïç</a> <a id="11422" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11408" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="11424" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11425" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6418" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="11430" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11397" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="11432" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11382" class="Bound">Œ≥</a><a id="11433" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11435" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="11437" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11208" class="Datatype">WHNF</a> <a id="11442" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11397" class="Bound">M</a>
<a id="11444" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11368" class="Function">ùïç‚ÜíWHNF</a> <a id="11451" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11452" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="11454" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11456" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4186" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="11458" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11458" class="Bound">x</a><a id="11459" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11461" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11462" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11462" class="Bound">v</a><a id="11463" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11465" class="Symbol">()</a>
<a id="11468" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11368" class="Function">ùïç‚ÜíWHNF</a> <a id="11475" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11476" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="11478" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11480" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∆õ</a> <a id="11482" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11482" class="Bound">N</a><a id="11483" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11485" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11486" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11486" class="Bound">v</a><a id="11487" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11489" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11489" class="Bound">vc</a> <a id="11492" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11494" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11245" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∆õ_</a>
<a id="11497" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11368" class="Function">ùïç‚ÜíWHNF</a> <a id="11504" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11505" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="11507" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11509" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11509" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="11511" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬∑</a> <a id="11513" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11513" class="Bound">M</a><a id="11514" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11516" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11517" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11517" class="Bound">v</a><a id="11518" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11520" class="Symbol">()</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Next we have an introduction rule for `ùïç` that mimics the `‚äî-intro`
rule. If both `u` and `v` are related to a closure `c`, then their join is
too.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="ùïç‚äî-intro"></a><a id="11697" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11697" class="Function">ùïç‚äî-intro</a> <a id="11706" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11708" class="Symbol">‚àÄ{</a><a id="11710" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11710" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="11712" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11712" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="11714" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11714" class="Bound">v</a><a id="11715" class="Symbol">}</a>
         <a id="11726" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="11728" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8984" class="Function">ùïç</a> <a id="11730" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11712" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="11732" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11710" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="11734" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="11736" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8984" class="Function">ùïç</a> <a id="11738" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11714" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="11740" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11710" class="Bound">c</a>
           <a id="11753" class="Comment">---------------</a>
         <a id="11778" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="11780" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8984" class="Function">ùïç</a> <a id="11782" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11783" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11712" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="11785" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4159" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚äî</a> <a id="11787" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11714" class="Bound">v</a><a id="11788" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11790" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11710" class="Bound">c</a>

<a id="11822" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11697" class="Function">ùïç‚äî-intro</a> <a id="11831" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11832" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6418" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="11837" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11838" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∆õ</a> <a id="11840" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11840" class="Bound">N</a><a id="11841" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11843" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11843" class="Bound">Œ≥</a><a id="11844" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11846" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11846" class="Bound">uc</a> <a id="11849" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11849" class="Bound">vc</a> <a id="11852" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11854" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü®</a> <a id="11856" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11846" class="Bound">uc</a> <a id="11859" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="11861" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11849" class="Bound">vc</a> <a id="11864" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a>
<a id="11866" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11697" class="Function">ùïç‚äî-intro</a> <a id="11875" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11876" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6418" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="11881" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11882" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11882" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="11884" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬∑</a> <a id="11886" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11886" class="Bound">M</a><a id="11887" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11889" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11889" class="Bound">Œ≥</a><a id="11890" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11892" class="Symbol">()</a> <a id="11895" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11895" class="Bound">vc</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

In a moment we prove that `ùïç` is preserved when going from a greater
value to a lesser value: if `ùïç v c` and `v' ‚äë v`, then `ùïç v' c`.
This property, named `ùïç-sub`, is needed by the main lemma in
the case for the `sub` rule.

To prove `ùïç-sub`, we in turn need the following property concerning
values that are not greater than a function, that is, values that are
equivalent to `‚ä•`. In such cases, `ùïç v (clos (∆õ N) Œ≥')` is trivially true.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="not-AboveFun-ùïç"></a><a id="12362" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12362" class="Function">not-AboveFun-ùïç</a> <a The proofs of `ùïç-sub` and `ùîº-sub` are intertwined.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="sub-ùïç"></a><a id="12805" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12805" class="Function">sub-ùïç</a> <a id="12811" %}#12867" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="12891" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="12893" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12879" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12877" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="12900" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="12902" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9007" class="Function">ùîº</a> <a id="12904" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12879" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="12907" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12867" class="Bound">c</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We prove `ùïç-sub` by case analysis on the closure's term, to dispatch the
cases for variables and application. We then proceed by induction on
`v' ‚äë v`. We describe each case below.

    <a id="14662" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="14667" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4102" class="Function">AboveFun-‚äî</a> <a id="14678" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü®</a> <a id="14680" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#14614" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="14683" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="14685" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü®</a> <a id="14687" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#14621" class="Bound">w&#39;&#39;</a> <a id="14691" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="14693" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#14627" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="14696" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a> <a id="14698" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a>
<a id="14700" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="14704" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="14706" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">inj‚ÇÅ</a> <a id="14711" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#14711" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="14715" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14717" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Empty.html#360" class="Function">‚ä•-elim</a> <a id="14724" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14725" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="14739" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#14711" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="14743" class="Bound">naf2</a><a id="14747" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="14749" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="14753" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="14755" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">inj‚ÇÇ</a> <a id="14760" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#14760" class="Bound">af3</a> <a id="14764" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14766" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Empty.html#360" class="Function">‚ä•-elim</a> <a id="14773" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14774" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="14788" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#14760" class="Bound">af3</a> <a id="14792" class="Bound">naf3</a><a id="14796" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* Case `Bot‚äë`. We immediately have `ùïç ‚ä• (clos (∆õ N) Œ≥)`.

* Case `ConjL‚äë`.

        v‚ÇÅ' ‚äë v     v‚ÇÇ' ‚äë v
        -------------------
        (v‚ÇÅ' ‚äî v‚ÇÇ') ‚äë v

  The induction hypotheses gives us `ùïç v‚ÇÅ' (clos (∆õ N) Œ≥)`
  and `ùïç v‚ÇÇ' (clos (∆õ N) Œ≥)`, which is all we need for this case. 

* Case `ConjR1‚äë`.

        v' ‚äë v‚ÇÅ
        -------------
        v' ‚äë (v‚ÇÅ ‚äî v‚ÇÇ)

  The induction hypothesis gives us `ùïç v' (clos (∆õ N) Œ≥)`.

* Case `ConjR2‚äë`.

        v' ‚äë v‚ÇÇ
        -------------
        v' ‚äë (v‚ÇÅ ‚äî v‚ÇÇ)

  Again, the induction hypothesis gives us `ùïç v' (clos (∆õ N) Œ≥)`.

* Case `Trans‚äë`.

        v' ‚äë v‚ÇÇ   v‚ÇÇ ‚äë v
        -----------------
             v' ‚äë v

  The induction hypothesis for `v‚ÇÇ ‚äë v` gives us
  `ùïç v‚ÇÇ (clos (∆õ N) Œ≥)`. We apply the induction hypothesis
  for `v' ‚äë v‚ÇÇ` to conclude that `ùïç v' (clos (∆õ N) Œ≥)`.

* Case `Dist‚äë`. This case  is the most difficult. We have

        ùïç (v ‚Ü¶ w) (clos (∆õ N) Œ≥)
        ùïç (v ‚Ü¶ w') (clos (∆õ N) Œ≥)

  and need to show that 

        ùïç (v ‚Ü¶ (w ‚äî w')) (clos (∆õ N) Œ≥)
  
  Let `c` be an arbtrary closure such that `ùîº v c`.
  Assume `w ‚äî w'` is greater than a function.
  Unfortunately, this does not mean that both `w` and `w'`
  are above functions. But thanks to the lemma `AboveFun-‚äî`,
  we know that at least one of them is greater than a function.
  
  * Suppose both of them are greater than a function.  Then we have
    `Œ≥ ‚ä¢ N ‚áì clos L Œ¥` and `ùïç w (clos L Œ¥)`.  We also have `Œ≥ ‚ä¢ N ‚áì c‚ÇÉ` and
    `ùïç w' c‚ÇÉ`.  Because the big-step semantics is deterministic, we have
    `c‚ÇÉ ‚â° clos L Œ¥`. Also, from `ùïç w (clos L Œ¥)` we know that `L ‚â° ∆õ N'`
    for some `N'`. We conclude that `ùïç (w ‚äî w') (clos (∆õ N') Œ¥)`.

  * Suppose one of them is greater than a function and the other is
    not: say `AboveFun w` and `¬¨ AboveFun w'`. Then from
    `ùïç (v ‚Ü¶ w) (clos (∆õ N) Œ≥)`
    we have `Œ≥ ‚ä¢ N ‚áì clos L Œ≥‚ÇÅ` and `ùïç w (clos L Œ≥‚ÇÅ)`. From this we have
    `L ‚â° ∆õ N'` for some `N'`. Meanwhile, from `¬¨ AboveFun w'` we have
    `ùïç w' (clos L Œ≥‚ÇÅ)`. We conclude that
    `ùïç (w ‚äî w') (clos (∆õ N') Œ≥‚ÇÅ)`.
    

The proof of `sub-ùîº` is direct and explained below.

    <a id="16965" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="16970" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#16949" class="Bound">ùîºv</a> <a id="16973" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16974" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#3536" class="Function">AboveFun-‚äë</a> <a id="16985" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#16957" class="Bound">fv&#39;</a> <a id="16989" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#16952" class="Bound">v&#39;‚äëv</a><a id="16993" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="16995" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="16999" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="17001" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü®</a> <a id="17003" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17003" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="17005" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="17007" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü®</a> <a id="17009" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17009" class="Bound">M‚áìc</a> <a id="17013" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="17015" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17015" class="Bound">ùïçv</a> <a id="17018" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a> <a id="17020" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a> <a id="17022" class="Symbol">=</a>
      <a id="17030" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü®</a> <a id="17032" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17003" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="17034" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="17036" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü®</a> <a id="17038" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17009" class="Bound">M‚áìc</a> <a id="17042" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="17044" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12805" class="Function">sub-ùïç</a> <a id="17050" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17015" class="Bound">ùïçv</a> <a id="17053" class="Bound">v&#39;‚äëv</a> <a id="17058" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a> <a id="17060" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

From `AboveFun v'` and `v' ‚äë v` we have `AboveFun v`.  Then with `ùîº v c` we
obtain a closure `c` such that `Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚áì c` and `ùïç v c`. We conclude with an
application of `sub-ùïç` with `v' ‚äë v` to show `ùïç v' c`.


## Programs with function denotation terminate via call-by-name

The main lemma proves that if a term has a denotation that is above a
function, then it terminates via call-by-name. More formally, if
`Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v` and `ùîæ Œ≥ Œ≥'`, then `ùîº v (clos M Œ≥')`. The proof is by
induction on the derivation of `Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v` we discuss each case below.

The following lemma, kth-x, is used in the case for the `var` rule.

      <a id="20059" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü®</a> <a id="20061" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20032" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="20063" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="20065" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü®</a> <a id="20067" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20038" class="Bound">M‚áìc</a> <a id="20071" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="20073" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12805" class="Function">sub-ùïç</a> <a id="20079" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#20044" class="Bound">ùïçv</a> <a id="20082" class="Bound">v&#39;‚äëv</a> <a id="20087" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a> <a id="20089" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚ü©</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* Case `var`. Looking up `x` in `Œ≥'` yields some closure, `clos M' Œ¥`,
  and from `ùîæ Œ≥ Œ≥'` we have `ùîº (Œ≥ x) (clos M' Œ¥)`. With the premise
  `AboveFun (Œ≥ x)`, we obtain a closure `c` such that `Œ¥ ‚ä¢ M' ‚áì c`
  and `ùïç (Œ≥ x) c`. To conclude `Œ≥' ‚ä¢ x ‚áì c` via `‚áì-var`, we 
  need `Œ≥' x ‚â° clos M' Œ¥`, which is obvious, but it requires some
  Agda shananigans via the `kth-x` lemma to get our hands on it.

* Case `‚Ü¶-elim`. We have `Œ≥ ‚ä¢ L ¬∑ M ‚Üì v`.
  The induction hypothesis for `Œ≥ ‚ä¢ L ‚Üì v‚ÇÅ ‚Ü¶ v`
  gives us `Œ≥' ‚ä¢ L ‚áì clos L' Œ¥` and `ùïç v (clos L' Œ¥)`.
  Of course, `L' ‚â° ∆õ N` for some `N`.
  By the induction hypothesis for `Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v‚ÇÅ`,
  we have `ùîº v‚ÇÅ (clos M Œ≥')`.
  Together with the premise `AboveFun v` and `ùïç v (clos L' Œ¥)`,
  we obtain a closure `c'` such that `Œ¥ ‚ä¢ N ‚áì c'` and `ùïç v c'`.
  We conclude that `Œ≥' ‚ä¢ L ¬∑ M ‚áì c'` by rule `‚áì-app`.

* Case `‚Ü¶-intro`. We have `Œ≥ ‚ä¢ ∆õ N ‚Üì v ‚Ü¶ w`.
  We immediately have `Œ≥' ‚ä¢ ∆õ M ‚áì clos (∆õ M) Œ≥'` by rule `‚áì-lam`.
  But we also need to prove `ùïç (v ‚Ü¶ w) (clos (∆õ N) Œ≥')`.
  Let `c` by an arbitrary closure such that `ùîº v c`.
  Suppose `v'` is greater than a function value.
  We need to show that `Œ≥' , c ‚ä¢ N ‚áì c'` and `ùïç v' c'` for some `c'`.
  We prove this by the induction hypothesis for `Œ≥ , v ‚ä¢ N ‚Üì v'`
  but we must first show that `ùîæ (Œ≥ , v) (Œ≥' , c)`. We prove
  that by the lemma `ùîæ-ext`, using facts `ùîæ Œ≥ Œ≥'` and `ùîº v c`.

* Case `‚ä•-intro`. We have the premise `AboveFun ‚ä•`, but that's impossible.

* Case `‚äî-intro`. We have `Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì (v‚ÇÅ ‚äî v‚ÇÇ)` and `AboveFun (v‚ÇÅ ‚äî v‚ÇÇ)`
  and need to show `Œ≥' ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì c` and `ùïç (v‚ÇÅ ‚äî v‚ÇÇ) c` for some `c`.
  Again, by `AboveFun-‚äî`, at least one of `v‚ÇÅ` or `v‚ÇÇ` is greater than
  a function.

  * Suppose both `v‚ÇÅ` and `v‚ÇÇ` are greater than a function value.
    By the induction hypotheses for `Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v‚ÇÅ` and `Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v‚ÇÇ`
    we have `Œ≥' ‚ä¢ M ‚áì c‚ÇÅ`, `ùïç v‚ÇÅ c‚ÇÅ`, `Œ≥' ‚ä¢ M ‚áì c‚ÇÇ`, and `ùïç v‚ÇÇ c‚ÇÇ`
    for some `c‚ÇÅ` and `c‚ÇÇ`. Because `‚áì` is deterministic, we have `c‚ÇÇ ‚â° c‚ÇÅ`.
    Then by `ùïç‚äî-intro` we conclude that `ùïç (v‚ÇÅ ‚äî v‚ÇÇ) c‚ÇÅ`.

  * Without loss of generality, suppose `v‚ÇÅ` is greater than a function
    value but `v‚ÇÇ` is not.  By the induction hypotheses for `Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v‚ÇÅ`,
    and using `ùïç‚ÜíWHNF`, we have `Œ≥' ‚ä¢ M ‚áì clos (∆õ N) Œ≥‚ÇÅ`
    and `ùïç v‚ÇÅ (clos (∆õ N) Œ≥‚ÇÅ)`.
    Then because `v‚ÇÇ` is not greater than a function, we also have
    `ùïç v‚ÇÇ (clos (∆õ N) Œ≥‚ÇÅ)`. We conclude that `ùïç (v‚ÇÅ ‚äî v‚ÇÇ) (clos (∆õ N) Œ≥‚ÇÅ)`.
    
* Case `sub`. We have `Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v`, `v' ‚äë v`, and `AboveFun v'`.
  We need to show that `Œ≥' ‚ä¢ M ‚áì c` and `ùïç v' c` for some `c`.
  We have `AboveFun v` by `AboveFun-‚äë`,
  so the induction hypothesis for `Œ≥ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì v` gives us a closure `c`
  such that `Œ≥' ‚ä¢ M ‚áì c` and `ùïç v c`. We conclude that `ùïç v' c` by `sub-ùïç`.


## Proof of denotational adequacy

The adequacy property is a corollary of the main lemma.
We have `‚àÖ ‚ä¢ ∆õ N ‚Üì ‚ä• ‚Ü¶ ‚ä•`, so `‚Ñ∞ M ‚âÉ ‚Ñ∞ (∆õ N)`
gives us `‚àÖ ‚ä¢ M ‚Üì ‚ä• ‚Ü¶ ‚ä•`. Then the main lemma gives us
`‚àÖ ‚ä¢ M ‚áì c` for some `c`.

    <a id="23155" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="23160" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#17944" class="Function">‚Üì‚Üíùîº</a> <a id="23164" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10830" class="Function">ùîæ-‚àÖ</a> <a id="23168" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="23170" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#167" class="Field">proj‚ÇÇ</a> <a id="23176" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23177" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#23148" class="Bound">eq</a> <a id="23180" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7471" class="Function">`‚àÖ</a> <a id="23183" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23184" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4117" class="InductiveConstructor">‚ä•</a> <a id="23186" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚Ü¶</a> <a id="23188" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4117" class="InductiveConstructor">‚ä•</a><a id="23189" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="23193" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23194" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10142" class="InductiveConstructor">‚Ü¶-intro</a> <a id="23202" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10266" class="InductiveConstructor">‚ä•-intro</a><a id="23209" class="Symbol">))</a>
